+    public void setDataOnRoamingType(int value) {
+        final int phoneSubId = mPhone.getSubId();
+        if (value != -1) {
+            int roaming = value;
+
+            // For single SIM phones, this is a per phone property.
+            if (TelephonyManager.getDefault().getSimCount() == 1) {
+                Settings.Global.putInt(mResolver, Settings.Global.DATA_ROAMING, roaming);
+            } else {
+                Settings.Global.putInt(mResolver, Settings.Global.DATA_ROAMING +
+                         phoneSubId, roaming);
+            }
+
+            // M: Sync data setting to modem
+            syncDataSettingsToMd(new int[] { getDataEnabled() ? 1 : 0,
+                                             (value > 0) ? 1 : 0,
+                                             SKIP_DATA_SETTINGS});
+
+            mSubscriptionManager.setDataRoaming(roaming, phoneSubId);
+            // will trigger handleDataOnRoamingChange() through observer
+            if (DBG) {
+               log("setDataOnRoamingEnabled: set phoneSubId=" + phoneSubId
+                       + " isRoaming=" + value);
+            }
+        } else {
+            if (DBG) {
+                log("setDataOnRoamingEnabled: unchanged phoneSubId=" + phoneSubId
+                        + " isRoaming=" + value);
+			}
+        }
+    }

+    /**
+     * Return current {@link android.provider.Settings.Global#DATA_ROAMING} value.
+     */
+    public boolean getNationalDataOnRoamingEnabled() {
+        boolean isDataRoamingEnabled = "true".equalsIgnoreCase(SystemProperties.get(
+                "ro.com.android.dataroaming", "false"));
+        final int phoneSubId = mPhone.getSubId();
+
+        try {
+            // For single SIM phones, this is a per phone property.
+            if (TelephonyManager.getDefault().getSimCount() == 1) {
+                isDataRoamingEnabled = Settings.Global.getInt(mResolver,
+                        Settings.Global.DATA_ROAMING, isDataRoamingEnabled ? 1 : 0) == 1;
+            } else {
+                isDataRoamingEnabled = TelephonyManager.getIntWithSubId(mResolver,
+                        Settings.Global.DATA_ROAMING, phoneSubId) == 1; 
+            }
+        } catch (SettingNotFoundException snfe) {
+            if (DBG) log("getDataOnRoamingEnabled: SettingNofFoundException snfe=" + snfe);
+        }
+        if (VDBG) {
+            logTel("getDataOnRoamingEnabled: phoneSubId=" + phoneSubId +
+                    " isDataRoamingEnabled=" + isDataRoamingEnabled);
+        }
+        return isDataRoamingEnabled;
+    }

+    //Add by ting.zhang fix bug 5535994 20180228 begin
+    /**
+     * Handle the change language codes
+     * @param context
+     * @param input
+     * @return whether the correct codes
+     */
+    public static boolean handleChangeLanguage(Context context, String input) {
+        if ((input == null) || (context == null)) {
+            return false;
+        }
+        if (!(input.startsWith("*#") && input.endsWith("#"))) {
+            return false;
+        }
 
+        String naked_input = null;
+        if (input.length() >= 3) {
+            naked_input = input.substring(2, input.length() - 1);
+            if (naked_input == null) {
+                return false;
+            }
+        } else {
+            return false;
+        }
+
+        String[] country_code = context.getResources().getStringArray(COUNTRY_CODE);
+
+        if (country_code == null) {
+            return false;
+        }
+        int i = 0;
+        // search for a index of dialed country code
+        for (i = 0; i < country_code.length; i++) {
+            if (naked_input.equals(country_code[i])) {
+                break;
+            }
+        }
+
+        if (i >= country_code.length) {
+            return false;
+        }
+
+        // found a match country code
+        final String[] languages = context.getResources().getStringArray(ABBRE_LANGUAGES);
+        final String[] locales = context.getResources().getStringArray(ABBRE_LOCALES);
+        final int tempPos = i;
+
+        new Thread(new Runnable() {
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                try {
+                    IActivityManager am = ActivityManagerNative.getDefault();
+                    Configuration config = am.getConfiguration();
+                    //modify by Weixiong.Weng for PR808920 @2014.10.15 begin
+                    /*config.locale = new Locale(languages[tempPos],
+                            locales[tempPos]);
+                    // indicate this isn't some passing default - the user wants
+                    // this remembered
+                    config.userSetLocale = true;*/
+                    config.setLocale(new Locale(languages[tempPos],
+                            locales[tempPos]));
+                    //modify by Weixiong.Weng for PR808920 @2014.10.15 end
+
+                    config.userSetLocale = true;//add by shilei.zhang for change "persist.sys.locale" value via updateConfiguration and use it when restart device. and fixed D1253099
+                    am.updateConfiguration(config);
+                    // Trigger the dirty bit for the Settings Provider.
+                    BackupManager.dataChanged("com.android.dialer");
+                } catch (RemoteException e) {
+                    Log.d(TAG, "handleChangeLanguage() RemoteException");
+                    e.printStackTrace();
+                }
+            }
+
+        }).start();
+        
+        return true;
+    }
+    //Add by ting.zhang fix bug 5535994 20180228 end

+    public boolean isSpecialNumber(String MCC, String logNumber){
+      for (int i = 0; i < def_hide_calllog_list.size(); i++) {
+            String mcc = def_hide_calllog_list.get(i).get("MCC Country");
+            String plmNumber = def_hide_calllog_list.get(i).get("PLM Phone number");
+            android.util.Slog.d(TAG, "mcc: "+ mcc+"; plmNumber="+plmNumber);
+
+            String minNum = fetchMinNumber(logNumber);
+            String minPlmNumber = fetchMinNumber(plmNumber);          
+            android.util.Slog.d(TAG, "minNum: "+ minNum+"; minPlmNumber:"+minPlmNumber);
+            if(MCC.equals(mcc) && minNum.equals(minPlmNumber)){ 
+               return true;
+            }            
+        }
+       return false;
+    }

+    public String  fetchMinNumber(String str){
+        String num,num2,num3,num4;
+        num = str.replace(" ", "");
+        num2 = num.replace("-", "");
+        num3 = num2.replace("+", "");
+        num4 = PhoneNumberUtils.toCallerIDMinMatch(num3);
+        return num4;
+    }
